### 1. 文本校正和替换提示

**Author**: [ロホ](https://x.com/rojorojo46)  **Date**: 2026-01-09  **Language**: ja

> 以下是用于 Nano Banana Pro 的一个简单提示，用于纠正现有图像中乱码（mojibake）文本。它指示 AI 使用现有图像，并在指定位置（左上、左下、右上、右下）用特定的日语短语替换不正确的文本。

![文本校正和替换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143698104_7s6var_G-QhydHaMAAoape.jpg)

```
画像をそのまま使い、文字化けの文字を直してください。左上「{argument name="左上テキスト" default="今日は可愛い髪型したー！"}」左下「{argument name="左下テキスト" default="坂川陽香の1日"}」右上「{argument name="右上テキスト" default="まほぴょんさんがリクエストしてくれました"}」右下「{argument name="右下テキスト" default="今日のラッキーカラーピンク"}」
```

Next to each stickered clothing item, write its name in a soft pencil-style handwritten label, creating an aesthetic fashion-notebook look.

![图像编辑：背景和物体替换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509732810_7y627c_G70ahO5WUAAdJ__.jpg)

```
Replace the background with [{argument name="holiday theme background" default="Holiday theme background"}]. Change the person's outfit to [{argument name="outfit" default="Outfit"}]. The person is holding a [{argument name="object" default="Object"}]. Don't change the person's pose

Show me this photo as if a professional photographer captured it with proper lightly, color grading, depth of field. Also replace the background with {argument name="new background" default="jurassic dinosaur christmas time"}. The man is holding a {argument name="new object" default="dinosaur"}. Don't change the man's pose
```

### 18. Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-03  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 Nano Banana Pro 图像编辑提示，用于添加水平撕纸条，其内部可以在线条艺术、水墨画、人物渲染、彩铅、水彩或铅笔画风格之间切换，同时保留原始角色和场景。

![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909252272_9wbhhd_G7OpzpjbAAArAAS.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909263804_ixlq43_G7Op-C-bgAEuLoh.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909266159_7uv4sl_G7Op_5tboAAB-eW.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909269212_kro3sp_G7OqBr5bUAAGeIs.jpg)

```
task: "edit-image: add widened torn-paper layered effect"

base_image:
  use_reference_image: true
  preserve_everything:
    - character identity
    - facial features and expression
    - hairstyle and anatomy
    - outfit design and colors
    - background, lighting, composition
    - overall art style

rules:
  - Only modify the torn-paper interior areas.
  - Do not change pose, anatomy, proportions, clothing details, shading, or scene elements.

effects:
  - effect: "torn-paper-reveal"
    placement: "across chest height"
    description:
      - Add a wide, natural horizontal tear across the chest area.
      - The torn interior uses the style defined in `interior_style`.

  - effect: "torn-paper-reveal"
    placement: "lower abdomen height"
    description:
      - Add a wide horizontal tear across the lower abdomen.
      - The torn interior uses the style defined in `interior_style`.

interior_style:
  mode: {argument name="画風モード" default="line-art"}

  style_settings:
    line-art:
      palette: "monochrome"
      line_quality: "clean, crisp"
      paper: "notebook paper with subtle ruled lines"

    sumi-e:
      palette: "black ink tones"
      brush_texture: "soft bleeding edges"
      paper: "plain textured paper"

    figure-render:
      material: "PVC-like"
      shading: "semi-realistic highlights"
      paper: "plain smooth surface"

    colored-pencil:
      stroke_texture: "visible pencil grain"
      palette: "soft layered hues"
      paper: "rough sketchbook paper"

    watercolor:
      palette: "soft transparent pigments"
      blending: "smooth bleeding"
      edges: "soft contours"
      paper: "watercolor paper texture"

    pencil-drawing:
      graphite_texture: "visible pencil grain"
      shading: "smooth gradients"
      line_quality: "mixed sharp and soft"
      tone: "gray-scale"
      paper: "notebook paper with faint ruled lines"
```

[[Image Editing]] [[Watercolor Style]]

**Author**: [Rodolfo Quisberth](https://x.com/simplissimus_)  **Date**: 2026-04-06  **Language**: en

![Nano Banana 2 巴洛克风格肖像转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544751205_xjsoo6_HFOVGULaIAAHHE-.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 巴洛克风格肖像转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544751235_akxt6k_HFOVGUGbUAAJvxP.jpg)

![Nano Banana 2 巴洛克风格肖像转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544752285_cr6bmo_HFOVGT0XsAAuWfv.jpg)

```
“Using the ATTACHED REFERENCE IMAGE as the identity source, create an ultra-detailed Baroque-style portrait that preserves the subject’s exact facial identity, bone structure, proportions, and skin texture with absolute fidelity. The subject is positioned in a classical aristocratic portrait composition, facing slightly off-center with a calm yet intense expression, evoking psychological depth and authority. Lighting: dramatic chiaroscuro with strong directional key light from one side, deep shadow falloff, and subtle Rembrandt triangle lighting on the face. Background is dark, rich, and painterly, with soft gradients and minimal distractions. Wardrobe: opulent 17th-century aristocratic attire with luxurious fabrics such as velvet, silk, and brocade, featuring intricate embroidery, lace details, and gold accents. Materials must show realistic texture, weight, and light interaction. Rendering style: oil painting realism with visible brushwork, soft blending, micro-texture, and subtle canvas grain. Inspired by classical Baroque masters like Rembrandt. Camera & optics: medium close-up portrait, 50mm lens feel, shallow depth of field (f/1.8), sharp focus on eyes, smooth falloff. Color grading: warm golden tones, deep shadows, rich contrast, cinematic dynamic range. Focus on depth, realism, material fidelity, and emotional intensity. Ultra-high detail, museum-grade finish, rich painterly realism.”
```

    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",

      "grain": "fine_35mm",

      }

      }
    },
    "subject": {
      "person": "adult woman",

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-02-23  **Language**: en

```

  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",

      "preserve_hand_structure": true,

Maintain facial proportions, hairstyle (long dark hair with volume), and the blowing-kiss gesture toward camera (hand lifted near lips, eyes closed, lips puckered). Keep the strapless red satin dress silhouette and gold jewelry. Maintain the clean white wall background and strong direct-flash aesthetic with a crisp shadow behind her. Improve realism only: natural skin texture, accurate satin highlights, correct anatomy. No text, no logos, no watermark."
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,
      "sharpness": "editorial_crisp",
      "grain": "subtle",
      "color_grade": "clean_flash_contrast"
    },

      "environment": "minimal matte white wall studio",
      "composition": "tight 3/4 portrait; subject filling frame; maintain original crop",
      "lighting": {
        "style": "on-camera direct flash",
        "quality": "hard light",
        "shadow": "distinct hard shadow on wall",
        "notes": "avoid soft studio diffusion; keep authentic flash falloff"
      }
    },
    "camera": {
      "shot_type": "tight portrait",
      "camera_angle": "eye_level",
      "lens": "50mm prime",
      "aperture": "f/4",
      "shutter": "1/160",
      "iso": "200",
      "white_balance": "flash_daylight",
      "focus": "face and hand"
    },
    "subject": {
      "person": "adult woman",

      "makeup": "clean glam, defined lashes, soft blush, satin nude-rose lips",
      "hair": "dark, full volume, natural shine",

### 37. 老照片的图像到图像修复

**Author**: [なぁさん｜SNSで1億円](https://x.com/nasan_0422)  **Date**: 2026-02-10  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Gemini 应用的 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 格式提示，用于对受损老照片进行图像到图像的修复，重点是在实现逼真的现代肖像质量的同时，保留人物的身份和表情。

![老照片的图像到图像修复](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770792224610_pjfotk_HAwjogOaAAMe76t.jpg)
![老照片的图像到图像修复](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770792224624_u33owe_HAwjogPaAAEpKVg.jpg)

```
{
  "task": "image-to-image restoration",
  "input_image": "output_from_prompt_1",
  "reference_image": {
    "type": "face_reference",
    "description": "損傷した写真と同じ顔、アイデンティティは変更せずそのまま"
  },
  "restoration_settings": {
    "restore_face": true,
    "restore_skin_texture": true,
    "remove_damage": true,
    "preserve_expression": true,
    "preserve_pose": true
  },
  "image_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "2:3 portrait",
    "resolution": "8K ultra-HD",
    "color_mode": "natural warm color",
    "clarity": "high-end modern portrait"
  },
  "subject": {
    "pose": "損傷した写真から変更なし",
    "expression": "同じ穏やかな笑顔",
    "details": "自然な肌の質感、現実的な目、クリーンな髪のディテール"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "soft cinematic studio lighting",
    "quality": "均一で魅力的な、モダンなもの"
  },
  "background": {
    "style": "クリーンなニュートラルスタジオ背景",
    "look": "ソフトボケ、テクスチャ損傷なし"
  },
  "quality_targets": [
    "傷なし",
    "折れ目なし",
    "汚れなし",
    "ぼかしなし",
    "経年劣化の痕跡なし"
  ],
  "realism": "フォトリアリスティックなモダンポートレート写真",
  "negative_prompt": [
    "顔の変更",
    "アイデンティティの変更",
    "過度なスムージング",
    "プラスチックのような肌",
    "芸術的なイラスト風"
  ]
}

### 38. 老照片修复提示

**Author**: [Johnn](https://x.com/john_my07)  **Date**: 2026-02-09  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 对老旧照片进行图像到图像的修复，重点在于在去除损坏、划痕和老化痕迹的同时，保留人物的身份和表情，最终生成 8K 超高清的现代肖像。

![老照片修复提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706209124_wayuz2_HAsE4CdakAAJuGl.jpg)
![老照片修复提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706209235_yx05ha_HAsE4BtbcAAaVQs.jpg)

```
{
  "task": "image-to-image restoration",
  "input_image": "output_from_prompt_1",
  "reference_image": {
    "type": "face_reference",
    "description": "Same face as damaged photo, identity must remain unchanged"
  },
  "restoration_settings": {
    "restore_face": true,
    "restore_skin_texture": true,
    "remove_damage": true,
    "preserve_expression": true,
    "preserve_pose": true
  },
  "image_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "2:3 portrait",
    "resolution": "8K ultra-HD",
    "color_mode": "natural warm color",
    "clarity": "high-end modern portrait"
  },
  "subject": {
    "pose": "unchanged from damaged photo",
    "expression": "same gentle smile",
    "details": "natural skin texture, realistic eyes, clean hair detail"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "soft cinematic studio lighting",
    "quality": "even, flattering, modern"
  },
  "background": {
    "style": "clean neutral studio backdrop",
    "look": "soft bokeh, no texture damage"
  },
  "quality_targets": [
    "no scratches",
    "no folds",
    "no stains",
    "no blur",
    "no aging artifacts"
  ],
  "realism": "photorealistic modern portrait photography",
  "negative_prompt": [
    "face alteration",
    "identity change",
    "over-smoothing",
    "plastic skin",
    "artistic illustration look"
  ]
}
```

### 55. 刺客风格转换提示词（日文）

**Author**: [ちゃろん](https://x.com/charon_artist)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: ja

> 一个日文提示，用于将图像转换为“刺客风格”插画，强调月光下酷炫的外观，眼睛从兜帽下窥视。提示本身在 ALT 文本中提及，但未提供，因此内容是从主描述中提取的。

月夜に舞う影！

### 56. 精确姿态与构图复制提示

**Author**: [骑司Chase](https://x.com/qisi_ai)  **Date**: 2025-12-28  **Language**: zh

> 一个高度技术性的中文提示，专为图像到图像生成（Nano Banana Pro）设计，严格要求将参考图像的姿势、摄像机角度、构图和取景复制到来自不同源图像的主体上，同时禁止对主体的身份或风格进行任何更改。

![精确姿态与构图复制提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061668708_bwo6di_G9PclW2bgAEDApq.jpg)
![精确姿态与构图复制提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061669070_eco6p8_G9PcmH_bMAA6ifD.jpg)

```
一、核心目标与强约束
1 姿势精确复刻：以图二为姿势唯一参考，将图一人物的全身姿势进行“逐点对齐”复刻（头、颈、肩、胸、髋、膝、踝、手臂、手腕、手指的朝向与弯曲程度一致）。
2 视角与镜头一致：相机机位、拍摄角度、镜头高度、俯仰角、左右偏转角、透视关系、景深效果与图二一致。
3 构图一致：人物在画面中的位置、占比、留白比例、裁切方式（是否截到脚/头顶/手）与图二一致。
4 头部与视线一致：头部倾斜角度、下巴抬/收程度、视线方向与图二一致。
5 外观禁止改动：严格保留图一人物的身份特征与风格（脸型五官、发型发色、肤色、服装款式与颜色、材质、配饰、纹理、体型比例、年龄气质、画风/渲染风格），只改变姿势与镜头构图以匹配图二。

二、执行方式与校准要求
1 对齐方法：以图二人物骨架为“目标骨架”，将图一人物骨架“重定向”到目标骨架；四肢角度、重心位置、躯干扭转幅度必须匹配。
2 关键点优先级：先匹配重心与骨盆朝向，再匹配躯干旋转与肩线，再匹配四肢末端（手、脚），最后微调手指与表情细节。
3 允许变化范围：姿势与镜头的误差尽可能为0；若不可避免，误差必须极小且不可肉眼明显。
4 禁止项：禁止新增或删除物体；禁止改变服装造型与细节；禁止改变人物风格；禁止换背景风格导致构图变化；禁止把图二人物的外观特征迁移到图一人物身上。
```

[[Image-To-Image]]

---

> 这是一个图像到图像生成任务的提示，指示 AI 将上传的人物照片转换为一场高风险的掰手腕比赛。该提示要求保留主体的面部和表情，同时引入超现实的“大力水手”卜派（拥有巨大的前臂）作为对手，以及奥莉薇作为裁判。这是通过提示进行图像处理的创意用法。

Transform this photo into a high-stakes arm wrestling match. Keep the subject's face and expression exactly as they are, sitting at a wooden table, straining with effort.
The Opponent: Facing them is a hyper-realistic Popeye. He has normal human proportions except for his massive, bulging forearms which are bigger than his head. He is looking calm and winking.
The Referee: Olive Oyl is standing between them as the referee, looking lanky and tall, screaming 'GO!' with her arms flailing.
Style: Gritty bar lighting, wooden textures, focus on the contrast between the subject's arm and Popeye's giant arm

### 71. 基于参考图像的手绘素描插画

**Author**: [simeon-sanai](https://x.com/Naiknelofar788)  **Date**: 2026-04-05  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Gemini Nano Banana 2 编写的提示词，旨在将上传的图像转换为在横线记事本纸上的精细手绘插画，采用彩色铅笔和墨水风格，并带有漫画风格的注释与涂鸦。

![基于参考图像的手绘素描插画](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775458523998_kwm274_HFHBTAAaUAAdsHq.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded image as your main reference point. Keep the same pose, facial features, proportions, and composition of the person. Turn the image into a hand-drawn illustration on lined notepad paper. The character should look like a detailed drawing in colored pencil and ink with cross-hatching and shading of the sketch. Add comic book-style drawings and notes around the character, such as arrows, doodles, “WOW”, “COOL!”and design notes. Circle the character with the smooth red-yellow glow of the sketch. Keep the concentrated composition of the portrait and the proportions of the whole body as in the original photo.The style should be similar to a conceptual drawing from a designer sketchbook: playful doodles, rough lines, warm tones, high detail. concept art for a sketchbook, drawings of characters on sheets of paper, illustrations with colored pencils, a background made of paper for a notebook, design notes made by hand You can choose the aspect ratio depending on the artificial intelligence or design you are using.
```

### 72. 剪纸分层插画风格迁移

**Author**: [each::labs](https://x.com/eachlabs)  **Date**: 2026-04-01  **Language**: en

> 一个用于 Nano Banana Pro Edit 的提示词，可将上传的照片转换为柔和的手工剪纸分层插画，强调柔和的配色方案、层与层之间的视觉深度以及主体人物周围清晰的白色轮廓。

![剪纸分层插画风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112280076_lgq0p5_HE0YSvaWsAA-lR4.jpg)
![剪纸分层插画风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112280065_h1r680_HE0YWJDacAAl9nO.jpg)
![剪纸分层插画风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112280090_5wjgiu_HE0YZjGbEAA1FRl.jpg)
![剪纸分层插画风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112280722_g0myz9_HE0YaQAWwAAsmUH.jpg)

```
Convert this image into a soft, handcrafted paper-cut layered illustration style, inspired by papercraft diorama aesthetics. Use smooth rounded shapes, simplified cute character proportions, and minimal facial details (dot eyes, blush cheeks) to create a warm, charming look. Apply stacked paper layers with visible depth, subtle shadows between layers, and clean cut edges that resemble laser-cut cardstock. 
Add a distinct white outer outline layer surrounding each main character, resembling a thick sticker border or white cut-paper backing, clearly separating the characters from the background. This white layer should feel like an intentional paper layer, not a glow.

Use a pastel color palette with muted blues, greens, and warm neutrals, balanced and calming.

Lighting should feel soft, diffused, and even, enhancing the dimensional paper layers without harsh contrast. Textures should appear matte and tactile, like thick art paper or craft foam.

Overall mood: cozy, wholesome, gentle, and

storybook-like, with a playful yet polished handcrafted feel suitable for modern illustration, children's books, or decorative art.
```

### 73. 电影级都市街头风格改造提示

**Author**: [Aegon](https://x.com/Fujimoto_hina)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: en

> 一个用于图像生成的复杂 JSON 提示，要求将上传的基础图像转换为电影级、超写实的街头风格照片，其中包含同一角色的卡通/Q 版插画版本，并强调特定的服装、场景细节和技术渲染规格。

![电影级都市街头风格改造提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469795549_0zmvzt_HDP-qC0aEAElopa.jpg)
![电影级都市街头风格改造提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469795561_f6ofbx_HDP-qFzbQAEl4vJ.jpg)

```
{
"prompt_analysis": {
"output_format": "JSON",
"request_type": "Image generation transformation and scene description",
"base_image_reference": "[UPLOAD YOUR IMAGE]",
"desired_output": {
"style": "64K DSLR-quality ultra-hyperrealistic cinematic outdoor street-style photograph, mixed media (photography + cartoon illustration), Instagram aesthetic, playful urban vibe",
"main_subject": {
"description": "Stylish man, same face as base image, confident relaxed vibe",
"hair": "Short dark hair, well-groomed beard",
"accessories": ["Thin metal-frame black round sunglasses"],
"attire": {
"jacket": "{argument name=\"jacket color\" default=\"Red\"} leather jacket",
"layer": "White shirt with a red tie",
"trousers": "Cream-colored wide-leg trousers",
"shoes": "Black leather shoes",
"details": ["Small keychain accessory hanging from belt loop"]
},
"pose": "Leaning casually against a tall metal pole, one leg crossed over the other, looking slightly to the side"
},
"secondary_subject": {
"style": "Cartoon / chibi-style illustrated version of the same character, exaggerated cute proportions",
"relationship": "Mirrors the real person's outfit and pose, leaning against the same pole on the other side",
"attire_match": {
"hair": "Curly hair (cartoon style)",
"accessories": ["Sunglasses"],
"jacket": "Red jacket",
"shirt": "White shirt",
"tie": "Tie",
"trousers": "Cream trousers",
"shoes": "Black shoes"
},
"purpose": "Playful comparison between real-life fashion and animated character design"
},
"scene_details": {
"setting": "Clean urban sidewalk, light stone tiles",
"background": "Modern glass building, large glass windows, minimalist design",
"lighting": "Bright daylight, natural sunlight with soft shadows",
"atmosphere": "Trendy social media aesthetic"
},
"technical_specifications": {
"camera_look": "50mm lens",
"depth_of_field": "Shallow",

```
Reinterpret the uploaded image as a structure carved from cooled volcanic lava rock. Preserve the main subject, silhouette, proportions, and recognizable structure of the original image, but transform all surfaces into porous basalt stone. The subject appears sculpted from hardened lava with rough textures, volcanic pores, cracks, and irregular rock surfaces typical of basalt formations. Some areas show subtle glowing embers deep within cracks while most of the rock appears dark and cooled. The environment feels volcanic and rugged with dramatic lighting emphasizing the texture of the stone. Cinematic geological photography, high detail, strong shadows, tactile rock textures. Negative constraints: no readable text, no letters, no numbers, no logos, no duplicated objects, no smooth plastic surfaces, no cartoon rendering style.

### 84. 黑白纪录片拥抱电影剧照提示

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-02-15  **Language**: en

> 一个高度受控的 JSON 提示，用于生成一对亲密情侣拥抱的黑白电影剧照。它使用图生图模式，严格保留身份和姿势，重点关注解剖学准确性（手、手指），并使用负面提示来避免常见的 AI 错误，例如长指甲或珠宝。

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "black_and_white_documentary_embrace_film_still",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.1_BW_INTIMATE_EMBRACE_NO_RING_SHORT_NAILS"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "very_high",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "preserve_pose": true,
      "preserve_hand_structure": true,
      "notes": "Use the reference image as the primary anchor. Keep the exact hugging pose, arm wrap, and body pressure. Remove any rings or jewelry from hands. Ensure nails are short, natural, and clean. Preserve identity and facial proportions without altering composition."
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "sharpness": "filmic_crisp",
      "grain": "true_35mm_film",
      "halation": "subtle",
      "contrast": "medium_high"
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "raw intimate embrace captured as a cinematic black-and-white film still",
      "environment": "simple interior room, minimal background",
      "lighting": {
        "style": "soft overhead practical + gentle side fill",
        "key_light": "dim soft overhead with natural falloff",
        "fill_light": "low fill to preserve skin texture",
        "shadow_behavior": "deep but not crushed"
      },
      "camera": {
        "lens": "50mm",
        "aperture": "f/2.0",
        "depth_of_field": "shallow focus on arms and embrace center",
        "framing": "tight mid-shot"
      }
    },
    "subjects": {
      "count": 2,
      "type": "adult couple",
      "pose": "tight hug, heads close, faces partially hidden",
      "hand_details": {
        "rings": "none",
        "jewelry": "none",
        "nails": "short, natural, unpolished"
      },
      "anatomy_rules": "accurate arm muscles, realistic grip pressure, correct finger count, natural wrist angles"
    },
    "style": {
      "color": "pure black and white",
      "look": "cinematic documentary",
      "texture": "visible pores and fabric weave",
      "motion": "still frame"
    },
    "quality_control": {
      "hands_priority": "maximum",
      "pose_lock": "strict",
      "jewelry_check": "remove rings completely",
      "avoid": [
        "extra fingers",
        "long nails",
        "painted nails",
        "rings",
        "bracelets",
        "deformed hands",
        "warped arms",
        "melted faces",
        "bad anatomy",
        "plastic skin",
        "text",
        "watermark",
        "logo"
      ]
    },
    "negative_prompt": [
      "rings",
      "long nails",
      "glossy manicure",
      "extra limbs",
      "distorted anatomy",
      "cartoon look",
      "heavy blur",
      "low resolution"
    ]
  }
}
```

> 这是一个为图生图生成设计的提示词，指示 AI 将上传的参考照片转换为吉卜力工作室风格的插画。它要求在保留主体身份和姿势的同时，应用吉卜力风格的特征：柔和的手绘线条、温暖的蜡笔色调、富有表现力的眼睛，以及带有柔和金色光芒的魔幻怀旧背景。

```
Create a Studio Ghibli–inspired illustration based on the uploaded reference image.
Preserve the person’s face structure, expression, gender, and pose exactly as in the original image.

Transform the art style into classic Ghibli animation:
– soft hand-drawn lines
– warm pastel color palette
– gentle anime proportions
– expressive eyes with natural emotions
– smooth skin texture, painterly shading

Environment:
Add a dreamy, peaceful Ghibli-style background that matches the mood of the image
(such as lush green fields, soft clouds, glowing sunlight, floating particles, or a cozy fantasy village).

Lighting & Mood:
– soft golden light
– calm, nostalgic, magical atmosphere
– cinematic anime feel

### 107. Image-to-Snowman Conversion Prompt for Nano Banana Pro

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度详细的提示，用于将参考图像中的角色转换为雪人水彩插画。它包含关于雪人结构的严格规则，排除了人类特征，并将头发材质渲染为纯白色、压实的雪。

![Image-to-Snowman Conversion Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237941688_na0hro_G8aiLeaakAICPKy.jpg)
![Image-to-Snowman Conversion Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237941961_kdzr20_G8aiNluakAIuZjR.jpg)

```
# ここに参照画像のキャラクターの人数、名前、外見の特徴を記述
[{argument name="キャラクターの外見" default="マントを羽織った少女とセーラー服の少女"}]

上記の全てのキャラクターが、それぞれかわいい「雪だるま（スノーマン）」の姿に変身した水彩画イラスト。

変換のルール:
- 全てのキャラクターの体は、白い雪の玉が重なった「手足のない雪だるま」の形状になる。
- 全身は2段または3段の雪玉で構成された雪だるま。等身の高いキャラクターは3段にする。
- 人間の肌、手足、服のディテールは排除し、雪のボディにする。
- 各キャラクターを識別するために、それぞれの特徴的な「帽子」「リボン」「イメージカラーのボタンやマフラー」のみを雪だるまに装着させる。
- 顔は雪だるま用のシンプルなパーツ（黒く丸い目、オレンジや丸い鼻）にする。

★材質の重要ルール（髪部分の修正）:
- 【最優先】髪の部分は絶対に「人間の髪」や「カツラ」として描画しないこと。
- 髪の形状は維持するが、材質は全て「真っ白な雪の塊」にする。
- 元のキャラクターの髪色（黒や茶色など）は完全に無視し、雪本来の「白一色（#FFFFFF）」で表現する。
- 髪の毛一本一本の線（ストランド）は描かず、雪を押し固めたような「ひとかたまりの物体」として描く。
- 頭部の雪玉と髪型部分の境界線をなくし、一つの大きな雪像（スノースカルプチャー）のように一体化させる。
- 質感は滑らかにせず、雪特有の「ざらつき」や「凹凸」を持たせる。
- 髪の形は、雪だるまの頭部と一体化した「白いシルエット」として描く。毛先は鋭くせず、溶けかけた雪のように丸く、ぼてっとしたフォルムにする。

アートスタイル:
- アナログ感のある水彩画。
- 白い画用紙のテクスチャ。
- 輪郭は柔らかく、色は淡く滲んでいる。
- 背景は白、またはうっすらとした雪景色。
```

[[Image-To-Image Generation]] [[Watercolor Illustration]]

**Author**: [✩ em ✩](https://x.com/promptprincess)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的系统提示，定义了一个 AI 角色（“时空假日工匠”），并要求它将参考图像重新渲染成从随机选择的历史时期（1850 年至 2060 年）的圣诞贺卡风格。它包括对时代保真度、文本内容和主题时尚的严格限制。

![Chrono-Holiday Artisan：Era 重新渲染的圣诞贺卡](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042072187_lyo63n_G8ZVF4zWYAAOxpP.jpg)
![Chrono-Holiday Artisan：Era 重新渲染的圣诞贺卡](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042073635_cyps3t_G8ZVHK5XgAEzplx.jpg)

```
ROLE: You are The Chrono-Holiday Artisan, a designer who exists outside of time, curating Christmas cards from every era of human history (1850–2060).

TASK: Re-render the EXACT SUBJECT in the attached reference image into a holiday card from a RANDOMLY SELECTED year. 

STRICT GUIDELINES:
1. THE ERA: Pick one random year (e.g., {argument name="example year 1" default="1894"}, {argument name="example year 2" default="1956"}, {argument name="example year 3" default="1982"}, {argument name="example year 4" default="2045"}) and strictly apply that era's specific printing technology, film grain, and color palette.
2. THE TEXT: Display ONLY a generic, period-accurate greeting (e.g., "Season's Greetings", "Merry Christmas", "Happy Holidays"). 
3. THE EXCLUSION: ABSOLUTELY NO names, NO "From the family", NO signatures.
4. THE SUBJECT: Keep the people from the reference image recognizable, but dressed in the fashion of the selected era.

--ar 3:4 --iw 2 --stylize 400

### 109. 详细的镜子自拍御宅族房间场景

**Author**: [宝玉](https://x.com/dotey)  **Date**: 2025-10-10  **Language**: zh

> 一个非常详细的 Nano Banana 提示，描述了一位女性在蓝色调御宅族电脑角拍摄的镜面自拍，包含角色、环境、灯光、相机和负面提示的完整规格。

![详细的镜子自拍御宅族房间场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763889946850_689z0h_G23i3sJW0AASGUw.jpg)

```
### **场景**
镜子自拍，御宅族电脑角落，蓝色调

---

### **主体**
* **性别表现**: 女性
* **年龄段**: 25岁左右
* **种族**: 东亚
* **身材**: 苗条，腰线分明；身材比例自然
* **肤色**: 浅中性色调
* **发型**:
    * **长度**: 及腰长发
    * **样式**: 直发，发尾微卷
    * **颜色**: 中等棕色
* **姿势**:
    * **站姿**: 站立，轻微的对立式平衡站姿（contrapposto）
    * **右手**: 手持手机挡住脸（身份被遮挡）
    * **左臂**: 在躯干旁自然下垂
    * **躯干**: 身体轻微后仰；露出腰腹
* **着装**:
    * **上衣**: 浅蓝色短款针织开衫，扣上前两颗纽扣；隐约可见蓝色法式内衣
    * **下装**: 牛仔超短裤，两侧臀部各有一个蓝色缎带蝴蝶结
    * **袜子**: 蓝白横条纹过膝长袜
    * **配饰**: 蓝色可爱吉祥物手机壳

---

### **环境**
* **描述**: 从挂墙镜中看到的卧室电脑角落
* **陈设**:
    * 白色书桌
    * 单显示器，显示着柔和的蓝色壁纸（没有可读的文字）
    * 机械键盘，白色键帽，放在蓝色桌垫上
    * 鼠标，放在小号蓝色鼠标垫上
    * PC主机在右侧，带有蓝色机箱灯效
    * PC主机上或附近有三个动漫手办
    * 墙上贴着一张佛塔海报
    * 猫形台灯，带有蓝色点缀
    * 一杯透明的玻璃水杯
    * 窗边（镜头左侧）有一株高大的绿叶植物
* **颜色替换**: 将所有原先的粉色元素（衣物和房间）替换为蓝色（婴儿蓝 -> 天空蓝/长春花蓝）。

---

### **灯光**
* **光源**: 来自镜头左侧大窗户的日光，透过薄纱窗帘
* **光线质感**: 柔和的漫射光
* **白平衡 (K)**: 5200

---

### **相机**
* **模式**: 智能手机后置摄像头通过镜子拍摄（无肖像/虚化模式）
* **等效焦距 (mm)**: 26
* **距离 (米)**:
    * 主体到镜子: 0.6
    * 相机到镜子: 0.5
* **曝光**:
    * 光圈 (f): 1.8
    * 感光度 (ISO): 100
    * 快门速度 (秒): 0.01
    * 曝光补偿 (EV): -0.3
* **对焦**: 对焦于镜中影像的躯干和短裤
* **景深**: 自然的智能手机景深（深景深）；背景清晰可辨，无人为模糊
* **构图**:
    * **宽高比**: 1:1
    * **裁剪**: 从头顶到大腿中部；画面包含书桌、显示器、PC主机和植物
    * **角度**: 从镜子的视角轻微俯拍
    * **构图备注**: 保持主体居中；为避免广角边缘拉伸，可以站远一些再进行方形裁剪

---

### **负面提示词**
* 任何地方出现粉色/品红色
* 美颜滤镜/磨皮皮肤；没有毛孔的外观
* 夸张或扭曲的人体结构
* NSFW，透视面料，走光
* 商标，品牌名，可读的用户界面文本
* 虚假的人像模式模糊，CGI/插画感
```

### 118. 伊斯坦布尔魅力女性的 Instagram 旅行九宫格

**Author**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin)  **Date**: 2026-04-03  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的结构化 JSON 提示词（并与 Grok Imagine 进行了对比），旨在创作一个 3x3 的 Instagram 九宫格，展示一位自然迷人、充满感性的女性在伊斯坦布尔各个标志性地点旅行的画面，呈现出随性自然的手机摄影风格。

![伊斯坦布尔魅力女性的 Instagram 旅行九宫格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284642069_p60qsd_HFAVW1UWEAAMpzZ.jpg)

```
{
  "objective": "Create a 3x3 Instagram feed grid featuring an attractive, sensual woman traveling in Istanbul, captured in natural smartphone-style photos",

  "aspect_ratio": "1:1",

  "composition": {
    "layout": "3x3 grid",
    "style": "Instagram travel feed",
    "spacing": "thin white borders",
    "consistency": "same woman across all images"
  },

    "appearance": {

      "build": "slim, feminine",
      "hair": "natural, slightly messy from wind",
      "expression": "relaxed, confident, candid"
    },
    "outfits": [
      "light summer dress",
      "linen shirt slightly unbuttoned",
      "flowy skirt or casual shorts",
      "sunglasses in some shots"
    ],
    "vibe": "effortless sensuality, not posed, candid travel moments"
  },

  "locations_and_shots": [
    {
      "location": "Sultanahmet / Hagia Sophia",
      "shot": "walking across square, sunlight hitting face"
    },
    {
      "location": "Blue Mosque courtyard",
      "shot": "looking up at architecture"
    },
    {
      "location": "Galata Tower",
      "shot": "leaning on railing, city behind"
    },
    {
      "location": "Kız Kulesi (Maiden’s Tower)",
      "shot": "sitting by the water, wind in hair"

      "location": "Bosphorus waterfront",

  "image_generation": {

      "pose": "standing, slightly leaning forward, one hand making peace sign, other hand holding a drink bottle",

        "tone": "fair",
        "texture": "smooth natural skin"

    },

      "bottom": "blue high-waisted jeans"
    },
    "accessories": [
      "white shoulder bag",
      "purple drink bottle with cute design"
    ],
    "environment": {
      "setting": "modern bakery shop",
      "background_elements": [
        "glass display with pastries and bread",
        "menu screens above counter",
        "warm yellow counter lighting",
        "staff working in background"
      ],
      "style": "clean modern cafe interior"
    },

    },

**Author**: [Sadie 🥀](https://x.com/NameIsSudee)  **Date**: 2026-04-01  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成高端时尚或生活方式人像的写实提示词，描绘了一位红发年轻女性坐在泳池边的场景，重点突出了薄荷绿泳衣、热带环境以及棕榈叶投下的斑驳光影效果。

{
  "image_prompt_details": {
    "subject": "Young woman with long, wavy {argument name="hair color" default="red"} hair and light freckles.",
    "clothing": "{argument name="swimsuit color" default="Mint green"} ribbed one-piece swimsuit with a scoop neckline.",
    "pose": "Sitting gracefully on light stone steps at the edge of a pool, legs crossed, leaning back slightly on one hand, looking off-camera with a soft, relaxed smile.",
    "environment": "Outdoor swimming pool with clear turquoise water, light travertine stone tiles, lush tropical greenery in the background, overhanging palm fronds framing the top right.",
    "lighting": "Bright, natural daytime sunlight, distinct dappled shadows from palm leaves falling across the subject's body and the stone ground.",
    "camera_and_style": "Photorealistic, high-end fashion or lifestyle photography, medium shot, shallow depth of field with a softly blurred background, vibrant but natural colors, highly detailed."
  },
  "full_prompt": "A photorealistic lifestyle portrait of a young woman with long, wavy red hair and light freckles wearing a mint green ribbed one-piece swimsuit. She is sitting gracefully on light travertine stone steps at the edge of an outdoor swimming pool with clear turquoise water. Her legs are crossed and she is leaning back slightly on one hand, looking off-camera with a soft, relaxed smile. The environment is a tropical oasis, featuring overhanging palm fronds that cast realistic dappled sunlight and shadows across her body and the stone tiles. In the background, there is lush greenery and a subtle stone wall, softly blurred with a shallow depth of field. High-end fashion photography, 8k resolution, highly detailed, vibrant natural lighting."
}

### 127. 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的随性手机照片提示

**Author**: [brindley](https://x.com/brindleyai)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张逼真的图像，模仿日常随手拍的智能手机照片。它详细说明了主题、环境、构图、相机设置（包括深景深和平视角度）、自然光照和纹理，目标是实现一种未经修饰、逼真的快照效果。

![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的随性手机照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421487919_lb2zea_HEKkH1sacAAHtWi.jpg)

```
{
  "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
  "photo_style": "casual everyday smartphone photo",
  "subject": "A woman with long, dark, wavy hair and braids, wearing a light blue camisole, sitting at a restaurant table. She is holding a fresh green coconut with a straw in one hand and holding a small piece of fruit to her mouth with the other.",
  "environment": "An airy, upscale indoor-outdoor restaurant or resort lounge with warm wood-paneled ceilings, large white pillars, and louvered windows. The furniture includes light-colored textured seating.",
  "composition": "A centered, waist-up medium shot taken from across the table. In the foreground, there is a white coffee cup on a saucer and a ceramic plate with slices of papaya, guava, and dragon fruit.",
  "camera": {
    "angle": "Eye-level",
    "distance": "Medium-close",
    "perspective": "Point-of-view from someone sitting across the table",

> 这是一个详细的提示词，用于通过 Nano Banana Pro 生成图像，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 将其转换为视频。该提示词旨在创建一个逼真、高质量的室内夜间 vlog 镜头，画面中一位女性正在讨论她的时尚，强调自然光线、温柔的表情和亲密的氛围。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

### 170. 在奢华衣帽间与狗狗的镜面自拍（图片和视频提示）

> 一套用于在奢华步入式衣帽间中生成逼真镜面自拍场景的双重提示（图像和视频）。图像提示详细说明了主体、服装、配饰（包括手机壳中的一张特定名人照片）和环境。视频提示则侧重于细微、逼真的动作，以实现电影般的动画效果。
